   \input tex4ht.sty    
   \Preamble{xhtml,th4,3,sections+}  \EndPreamble
   \input ProTex.sty          
   \AlProTex{c,<<<>>>,`,title,list,ClearCode,_^}

\input tex4ht-dir
\def\MYdir{\HOME texmf/tex4ht/ht-fonts}


\newwrite\dbcs     
\newwrite\unicode  

\let\coDE=\<
\def\<{\vfil\par\coDE}

\let\'=\Verb
\def\`{\expandafter\expandafter\expandafter\qts\Verb}
\def\qts#1{`#1\aftergroup'}

\def\AddFont#1#2{%
   \Comment{}{}\OutputCode[htf]\<#1\>%
   \let\StartDir=\empty  \def\EndDir{#2}\MakeDir
   \ifx \WWWdir\Undef \else
      \Needs{"cp #1.htf \WWWdir /#2.htf"}%
      \Needs{"chmod 644 \WWWdir /#2.htf"}%
   \fi
   \Needs{"mv #1.htf \MYdir /#2.htf"}%
   }
\def\MakeDir{\relax
   \expandafter \ifx  \csname !\StartDir\endcsname\relax
      \expandafter\let\csname !\StartDir\endcsname=\empty
      \Needs{"mkdir -p \MYdir/\StartDir"}%     
      \ifx \WWWdir\Undef \else
         \Needs{"mkdir -p \MYdir/\StartDir"}%     
         \Needs{"chmod 711 \WWWdir /StartDir"}%
      \fi
   \fi
   \ifx \EndDir\empty \else
       \expandafter\AppendDir \EndDir////*%
       \expandafter\MakeDir
   \fi
}
\def\AppendDir#1/#2/#3/*{%
   \def\temp{#2}\ifx \temp\empty  \let\EndDir=\empty 
   \else
      \edef\StartDir{\ifx \StartDir\empty\else \StartDir/\fi
                     #1}\def\EndDir{#2/#3}%
   \fi
}

\Needs{"mkdir -p \MYdir"}%

%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%

\newcount\tmpcnt  \tmpcnt\time  \divide\tmpcnt  60
\edef\temp{\the\tmpcnt}
\multiply\tmpcnt  -60 \advance\tmpcnt  \time

\edef\version{\the\year-\ifnum \month<10 0\fi
  \the\month-\ifnum \day<10 0\fi\the\day}

\def\CopyYear.#1.{%
   \ifnum #1=\year #1\space\space\space\space\space\space
    \else          #1--\the\year\fi
}

\CutAt{Section,Chapter}

\Chapter{Chinese, Japanese, Korean (CJK): GBSONG}
%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%


\<gbk2htf.c\><<<
/********************************************************************
 GBK2HTF Ver 1.0
 Translating gbk encoding file to htf fonts map file, which
    are used by TeX4HT
 Mar. 26, 2002
 Author: Eitan Gurari and Shengjun Zhong
 Now it can handle:
    gbksong01-gbksong24
    gbksong32-gbksong92
 The other fonts will be available in next version
********************************************************************/

#include <stdio.h>
#include <conio.h>
#include <string.h>
#include <stdlib.h>

// The ecodeing file path is "encode\*.*"
#define ENCODE_DIR "encode"

// The htf map file path, system
// #define HTF_DIR "d:\\localt~1\\tex4ht\\ht-fonts\\unicode\\cjk\\gbksong"

// The htf map file path, local
#define HTF_DIR "gbksong"

#define FONT_FAMILY "gbksong"

#define LEN_FILE_NAME 80
#define LEN_LINE 200

// Skip one line in a text file
void SkipOneLine(FILE *Handle)
{
 register int c;
 while((c=getc(Handle))!=EOF) if((char)c=='\n') return;
}

void GetFileNum(int fn,char *szfile)
{
 int n,d;
 szfile[2]=0;
 for(n=1;n>=0;n--)
   {
    d=fn%10;
    fn/=10;
    szfile[n]=d+'0';
   }
}

void ProcessFont(char *FontFamily,int Num,int dif)
{
    int j;
    int code,unicode;

 FILE *fp,*fpOut;
 char szTemp[LEN_LINE],szLine[LEN_LINE];
 char szTemp1[LEN_LINE],szTemp2[LEN_LINE];
 char InFile[LEN_FILE_NAME];
 char OutFile[LEN_FILE_NAME],FontName[LEN_FILE_NAME];

//  Get font name
    strcpy(FontName,FontFamily);
    GetFileNum(Num,szTemp);
    strcat(FontName,szTemp);

//  Get input file name
    strcpy(InFile,ENCODE_DIR);
    strcat(InFile,"\\");
    strcat(InFile,FontName);
    strcat(InFile,".enc");

//  Get output file name
    strcpy(OutFile,HTF_DIR);
    strcat(OutFile,"\\");
    strcat(OutFile,FontName);
    strcat(OutFile,".htf");

    printf("%s -> %s %x\n",InFile,OutFile,dif);

    fp=fopen(InFile,"rt");
    if(fp==NULL)
      {
       printf("Open file %s error",InFile);
       exit(1);
      }

    fpOut=fopen(OutFile,"wt");
    if(fpOut==NULL)
      {
       printf("Open file %s error",OutFile);
       exit(1);
      }
    fprintf(fpOut,"%s %d %d\n",FontName,0,255);

    strcpy(szTemp1,"/index");
    strcpy(szTemp2,"/.notd");

    // Skip the first line
    SkipOneLine(fp);

    // Process lines
    for(j=0;j<256;j++)
       {
        fgets(szLine,80,fp);
        strcpy(szTemp,szLine);
        szTemp[6]='\0';

        if( strcmp(szTemp,szTemp1) ==0 )
          {
           sscanf(&szLine[6],"%x",&code);
           unicode=code+dif;
           fprintf(fpOut,"%4s%4x%5s%4d\n","'&#x",unicode,";' ''",j);
          }
        else if( strcmp(szTemp,szTemp2) ==0 )
          {
           fprintf(fpOut,"%4s%4s%5s%4d\n","''","","''",j);
          }
        else
          {
           printf("Error! %s, unexpected line fond",szLine);
           break;
          }
       }
    fprintf(fpOut,"%s %d %d\n",FontName,0,255);

    fclose(fp);
    fclose(fpOut);
    return;
}


main()
{
 register int i;

 char doscommand[80];
 // Totally 94 fonts
 // Let waste a position so the position is used directly!
 int encode[95],unicode[95],dif[95];

 // Make directory for htf fonts
 strcpy(doscommand,"md ");
 strcat(doscommand,HTF_DIR);
 system(doscommand);

 // Set flags , means not defined
 for(i=1;i<=94;i++)
    {
     encode[i]=-1;
     unicode[i]=encode[i];
     dif[i]=0;
    }

 // Here are logic of some fonts files
 for(i=1;i<=94;i++)
   {
    if(i>=1 && i<=24 || i>=32 && i<=92)
       {
        // Tested!
        dif[i]=0x4a2c;
       }
   }

 // Please specify the encode and unicode of any font in a font file

 // Process all fonts files
 for(i=1;i<=94;i++)
    {
     // Try get dif from encode and unicode, if dif is not defined
     if(dif[i]==0)
        dif[i]=unicode[i]-encode[i];
     // if dif is defined eather explicitly,
     //    or by defining encode and unicode
     if(dif[i]!=0)
         ProcessFont("gbksong",i,dif[i]);
    }
 return 0;
}

>>>

%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%5




\def\EndCJK{%
   \CloseCode
   \Configure{charset}{charset=iso-8859-1}
}

\Configure{charset}{charset=big5}    


\def\GbkAlias#1#2{%
     \def\CURR{#1\ifnum\GBK<10 0\fi\GBK}
     \def\curfnt{#1}\def\tmp{gbkhei}\ifx \curfnt\tmp
       \leavevmode
           \special{t4ht>\CURR.log}%
            \special{t4ht=htfcss: 
                \CURR\space font-family: }\HChar{186}\HChar{218}%
            \HChar{204}\HChar{229}\special{t4ht=, sans-serif;}\hfill\break
            \special{t4ht<\CURR.log}
        \Needs{"mv \CURR.htf tmp; cat tmp \CURR.log > \CURR.htf; rm \CURR.log"}
      \fi
     \immediate\write\dbcs{\string\<\CURR\string\><<<}
     \immediate\write\dbcs{.gbksong\ifnum\GBK<10 0\fi\GBK}
     \immediate\write\dbcs{#2}
     \immediate\write\dbcs{>>>   
     \string\AddFont{\CURR}{alias/gbk/#1/\CURR}}
  \ifnum \GBK<94
    \HAdvance\GBK by 1 
    \def\next{\GbkAlias{#1}{#2}}%
    \expandafter\next
  \fi 
 }


\def\SECTION#1#2{
   \HAssign\GBK=1
   \def\Section{gbk#1}
   \GbkAlias{#1}{#2}}


\immediate\openout\dbcs=dbcs.log

  \SECTION{gbkcy}{htfcss: \CURR\space font-family:fantasy;}
  \SECTION{gbkfs}{htfcss: \CURR\space font-style: italic;}
%  \SECTION{gbkhei}{htfcss: \CURR\space font-family: &#186;&#218;&#204;&#229;, sans-serif;}
  \SECTION{gbkhei}{}
  \SECTION{gbkkai}{htfcss:
        \CURR\space font-family: monospace; font-style: italic;}
  \SECTION{gbkli}{htfcss: 
        \CURR\space  font-weight: bold; font-variant: small-caps;}
  \SECTION{gbkshu}{htfcss: \CURR\space  font-weight: bold;}
  \SECTION{gbksu}{htfcss: \CURR\space font-family:cursive;}
  \SECTION{gbkxh}{htfcss: \CURR\space font-family: monospace;}
  \SECTION{gbkxk}{htfcss: \CURR\space font-family:cursive; font-weight: bold;}
  \SECTION{gbkxw}{htfcss: \CURR\space  font-weight: bold; font-style: italic;}
  \SECTION{gbkyao}{htfcss:
         \CURR\space font-family: monospace; font-weight: bold;}
  \SECTION{gbkyou}{}

\immediate\closeout\dbcs
\input dbcs.log




%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%
\Chapter{Chinese, Japanese, Korean (CJK): Big5ka}
%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%


%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%
\def\EndCJK{%
   \CloseCode
   \Configure{charset}{charset=iso-8859-1}
}

\Configure{charset}{charset=big5}    


\def\SECTION#1{%
  \def\csec{b5ka12#1}\Section{b5ka12#1}
  \immediate\openout\dbcs=dbcs.log
  \immediate\openout\unicode=unicode.log
% NEW
     \immediate\write\dbcs{\string\<ntufsm#1\string\><<<}
     \immediate\write\dbcs{.b5ka12#1}
     \immediate\write\dbcs{>>>  
     \string\AddFont{ntufsm#1}{alias/cjk/b5ka/ntufsm#1}}
%
  \immediate\write\dbcs{\string\<b5ka12#1\string\><<<}
  \immediate\write\unicode{\string\<b5ka12#1-uni\string\><<<}
  \immediate\write\dbcs{b5ka12#1 0 255}
  \immediate\write\unicode{b5ka12#1 0 255}
 }

\parindent=0pt
\HAssign\CJKI=0
\HAssign\CJKJ=0
\HAssign\CJKK=0


\def\CloseCode{\ifx \csec\Undef\else
     \immediate\write\dbcs{\csec\space 0 255}
     \immediate\write\unicode{\csec\space 0 255}
     \immediate\write\dbcs{>>>  
            \string\AddFont{\csec}{dbcs/cjk/b5ka/\csec}}
      \immediate\write\unicode{>>>   
         \string\AddFont{\csec-uni}{unicode/cjk/b5ka/\csec}   } 
     \immediate\closeout\dbcs
     \immediate\closeout\unicode
     \input dbcs.log
     \input unicode.log
     \let\csec=\UnDef
  \fi}


\def\xx#1#2{%
   \ifnum \CJKJ=0
  \ifnum \CJKK>0  \CloseCode  \fi
   \ifcase \CJKK       \SECTION{01}  %0
              \or   \SECTION{02}        %1
             \or \SECTION{03}
             \or \SECTION{04}
             \or \SECTION{05}
             \or \SECTION{06}
             \or \SECTION{07}
             \or \SECTION{08}
             \or \SECTION{09}
             \or \SECTION{10}
             \or \SECTION{11}
             \or \SECTION{12}
             \or \SECTION{13}
             \or \SECTION{14}
             \or \SECTION{15}
             \or \SECTION{16}
             \or \SECTION{17}
             \or \SECTION{18}
             \or \SECTION{19}
             \or \SECTION{20}
             \or \SECTION{21}
             \or \SECTION{22}
             \or \SECTION{23}
%             \or \SECTION{28}
%             \or \SECTION{32}
%             \or \SECTION{38}
             \or \SECTION{24}
             \or \SECTION{25}
             \or \SECTION{26}
             \or \SECTION{27}
             \or \SECTION{28}
             \or \SECTION{29}
             \or \SECTION{30}
             \or \SECTION{31}
             \or \SECTION{32}
             \or \SECTION{33}
             \or \SECTION{34}
             \or \SECTION{35}
             \or \SECTION{36}
             \or \SECTION{37}
             \or \SECTION{38}
             \or \SECTION{39}
             \or \SECTION{40}
             \or \SECTION{41}
             \or \SECTION{42}
             \or \SECTION{43}
             \or \SECTION{44}
             \or \SECTION{45}
             \or \SECTION{46}
             \or \SECTION{47}
             \or \SECTION{48}
             \or \SECTION{49}
             \or \SECTION{50}
             \or \SECTION{51}
             \or \SECTION{52}
             \or \SECTION{53}
             \or \SECTION{54}
             \or \SECTION{55}
%
              \or   \section{??}        %2
   \else \fi \fi
   %%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%
   \def\temp{#1}\ifx \temp\empty \OTHER{}{}
   \else \def\tempa{?}\ifx \temp\tempa \OTHER{?}{}
   \else
      [\dd #1%
      \HCode{&\#\csname :gobble\endcsname#2;}]
      \ifx \csec\UnDef \else
          \immediate\write\unicode{'&\#\csname :gobble\endcsname#2;' ''
              \CJKln{(unicode)}}\fi
   \fi \fi
   %%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%
   \HAdvance\CJKJ by 1
   \HAdvance\CJKI by 1
   \ifnum \CJKI=8 \space :\CJKJ\HCode{<br/>}\HAssign \CJKI=0 
   \ifnum \CJKJ=256 \par \HCode{<hr />}\par
           \HAdvance\CJKK by 1 \HAssign\CJKJ=0 \fi
\fi}


\def\OTHER#1#2{      
      [#1]
      \ifx \csec\UnDef \else
          \immediate\write\unicode{'#1' '#2' \CJKln{(unicode)}}%
          \immediate\write\dbcs{'#1' '#2' \CJKln{(dbcs)\space\space\space}}%
      \fi}

\def\CJKln#1{%
  \ifnum \CJKJ<10 \space\fi
              \ifnum \CJKJ<100 \space\fi \CJKJ
  \ifcase\CJKJ 
        `space\%\%\%\%\%\%\%\%\%\%\%\%\%\%\%\%\%\%\%\%\%\%\%%
               \%\%\%\%\%\%\%\%\%\%\%\%\%\%\%\%\%\%\%\%\% %0
     \or\space \% \csec.htf #1 `space `space `space           `version \%    %1
     \or\space \% Copyright (C) `CopyYear.2000. Eitan M. Gurari \%    %2
     \or\space `<version 2`>    %3
     \or\space `<version 3`>    %4
     \or\space `<version 4`>    %5
     \or\space `<version 5`>    %6
     \or\space `<version 6`>    %7
     \or\space `<version 7`>    %8
     \or\space `<version 8`>    %9
     \or\space `<version 9`>    %10
     \or\space `<version 10`>    %11
     \or\space `<version 11`>    %12
     \or\space `<version 12`>    %13
     \or\space `<version 13`>    %14
     \or\space `<version 14`>    %15
     \or\space `<version 15`>    %16
     \or\space `<version 16`>    %17
     \or\space `<version 17`>    %18
     \or\space `<version 18`>    %19
  \else
  \fi
}


\bgroup
\catcode`\/=0 \catcode`\\=12
/gdef/bs{\}
/egroup

\def\dd#1#2#3#4#5#6{\ddd#3#4\let\SAVE=\CJKA
   \ddd#5#6\relax 
   \ifx \csec\UnDef \else
       \immediate\write\dbcs{'\bs\SAVE\bs\bs \CJKA\bs' '' 
           \CJKln{(dbcs)\space\space\space}}\fi
   }
\def\ddd#1#2{%
   \HAssign\CJKA=\CC#1\HMultiply\CJKA by 16 \HAdvance\CJKA by \CC #2%
   \HChar\CJKA}
\def\CC#1{%
    \if #100\fi
    \if #111\fi
    \if #122\fi
    \if #133\fi
    \if #144\fi
    \if #155\fi
    \if #166\fi
    \if #177\fi
    \if #188\fi
    \if #199\fi
    \if #1A10\fi
    \if #1B11\fi
    \if #1C12\fi
    \if #1D13\fi
    \if #1E14\fi
    \if #1F15\fi}
